# Higham Chapter 16 Source Coverage Ledger

## Source and Scope

- Edition: Higham, *Accuracy and Stability of Numerical Algorithms*, 2nd ed. (SIAM, 2002), verified from `pdfinfo` title metadata and source DOI path.
- Chapter: 16, "The Sylvester Equation".
- Printed pages read: 305-319.
- Source file: `References/1.9780898718027.ch16.pdf`.
- Mode: core.
- Parallel split: 3B.
- Planning documents consulted: `chapter_splitting/HIGHAM_PARALLEL_FORMALIZATION_BLUEPRINT.md`, the Split 3B section of `chapter_splitting/split_primary_contracts.md`, and the Chapter 16 rows of `chapter_splitting/chapter_index.md`.
- Selected-scope gate: FAIL. Several central square-Frobenius results, the rectangular vec/Kronecker formulation, the diagonal (16.3) coefficient/solution foundation including separated coefficient bijectivity, common-entry singularity, sigma-min bounds, Gram-eigenvalue lower-bound certificates, determinant/nonsingularity consequences, and the concrete-left-inverse/op-norm route to coefficient/operator lower bounds are proved, including general Sylvester concrete-left-inverse and finite-Gram-eigenvalue routes to `SepLowerBound` and exact `sylvesterSepInf`. Conditional exact Schur-coordinate transform plus supplied diagonal-factor and triangular-factor solve/vectorized-coefficient/determinant bridges are proved, the real quasi-Schur factor existence and exact transform solution-equivalence surfaces are recorded, and the real quasi-triangular route now has a supplied adjacent two-column exact block-system lemma, block-vector coefficient equivalence, supplied inverse/left-inverse certificates for the two active block columns, previous-column recurrence uniqueness wrappers, right-inverse/left-inverse solve uniqueness wrappers, inverse-consistency wrappers, determinant/surjectivity/bijectivity consequences, and an active-block unique-solve theorem. The Frobenius/`vec` norm bridge, coefficient sigma-min wrappers, product-index Gram-eigenvalue bridges for Sylvester and Lyapunov operators, exact Sylvester and Lyapunov `sylvesterSepInf` condition routes from both left-inverse and Gram data, supplied spectral-diagonal Lyapunov operator/coefficient/Gram lower-bound and `sep(A,-A^T)` lower-bound/source-shaped condition routes, the concrete-left-inverse and Gram Lyapunov sigma-min, sep, exact-infimum, first-order condition, condition-certificate witness, first-order wrappers, entrywise-gap first-order wrappers, and perturbation routes, the Sylvester Psi Gram certificate witness, the Lyapunov structured eta feasible-set/infimum model, the two-sided Lyapunov eta/xi infimum bridge plus attained minimizer, and the (16.29) practical max-entry/computed-residual budget bridge including raw and packaged monotone budget wrappers, scalar cap wrappers, generic residual-error-model wrappers, arbitrary-coefficient floating-point residual wrappers from supplied inverse certificates, a separated-diagonal floating-point scalar wrapper plus componentwise, monotone, and monotone scalar caps, and supplied diagonal/Schur-diagonal/Schur-triangular exact-inverse subcases with raw-budget, scalar, monotone, and monotone-scalar caps are proved. The full core pass still has open selected rows for the fully general Kronecker spectra/eigenvalue criterion, full block-nonsingularity/Hessenberg-Schur solve surfaces, floating-point stability beyond residual arithmetic, exact automatic condition-number formulas, rounded Schur solve/residual arithmetic, and LAPACK-style estimator paths.
- Latest selected-scope additions: certificate raw computed-residual budget endpoints now also have scalar, monotone, and monotone-scalar variants for concrete-left-inverse, finite-Gram, and sigma-min hypotheses; strict-block-map real quasi-Schur factors now instantiate the raw computed-residual practical bound for the original coordinates; exact vectorized Sylvester and Lyapunov coefficient solutions are identified with the nonsingular-inverse solution under determinant, sigma-min, finite-Gram, and concrete-left-inverse certificates; strict real-quasi-Schur block-label hypotheses turn the Schur factor into the supplied triangular case and yield original-coordinate uniqueness from shifted determinant certificates; Sylvester and Lyapunov vec coefficients expose both nonsingular-inverse left and right actions under determinant, sigma-min, finite-Gram, and concrete-left-inverse certificates; concrete-left-inverse, Gram, and sigma certificates instantiate non-floating raw computed-residual budget practical endpoints; real quasi-Schur factors feed directly into the repository's exact Schur-coordinate Sylvester solution equivalence; determinant-nonzero square Sylvester vec coefficients instantiate raw computed-residual budget, monotone, scalar, and monotone-scalar practical endpoints; determinant/sigma-min/finite-Gram/concrete-left-inverse certificates expose explicit nonsingular-inverse solve actions for Sylvester and Lyapunov vec coefficients; entrywise gap hypotheses produce determinant/nonsingularity certificates for diagonal and supplied Schur-diagonal Sylvester coefficients plus diagonal and supplied spectral-diagonal Lyapunov coefficients; square Sylvester determinant, Gram, sigma-min, and concrete-left-inverse finite-op-norm certificates instantiate scalar, monotone, and monotone-scalar floating-point practical residual endpoints with the nonsingular inverse; the non-floating computed-residual and explicit error-model practical endpoints also have determinant-nonzero square coefficient variants; generic determinant and concrete-left-inverse finite-op-norm certificates yield finite-matrix, Sylvester, and Lyapunov vectorized bijectivity and unique-solve wrappers; and nonsingular shifted triangular column coefficients expose inverse, injectivity, surjectivity, bijectivity, unique-solve, active column-step, and column-step equality wrappers for the triangular recurrence.

- Latest Lyapunov sigma-min source alias wave: the direct Lyapunov operator sigma-min route now exposes `H16_eq16_26_SepLowerBound_lyapunov_of_sigmaMin` and `H16_eq16_26_sylvesterSepInf_lyapunov_ge_of_sigmaMin`, making the (16.26) source map explicit for `sep(A,-A^T)` lower-bound certificates.
- Latest source absolute monotone/quasi-Schur block-system alias wave: source `SepLowerBound` and positive exact-infimum certificates now instantiate the denominator-free absolute monotone computed-residual certificate endpoints, quasi-Schur/no-coupled-action data now constructs supplied two-column block systems and previous-column uniqueness from nonsingular-inverse columns, and operator/source residual-budget endpoints now expose additional (16.29) aliases. These remain certificate-transfer wrappers rather than rounded Schur solve or estimator proofs.
- Latest degenerate same-block quasi-Schur determinant wave: same-block quasi-Schur block-map data plus two shifted determinant certificates and zero coupling product now packages the adjacent two-column predicate together with determinant nonsingularity through `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_block_and_det_ne_zero_of_quasiSchur_shifted_det_product_zero`. This closes the zero-coupling adapter subcase while leaving the genuinely coupled real-Schur block separation/no-coupled-action certificate open.
- Latest degenerate same-block solve-wrapper wave: the zero-coupling same-block quasi-Schur route now feeds active-block injectivity, surjectivity, bijectivity, trivial-kernel, unique-solve, nonsingular-inverse solution-identification, supplied two-column block-system construction, and previous-column uniqueness wrappers. These remain exact certificate-transfer facts for the degenerate subcase; they do not derive the coupled real-Schur separation certificate.
- Latest real-Schur source-numbered alias wave: the real quasi-Schur factor-existence surface and the exact original-to-Schur-coordinate Sylvester equivalence now expose `H16_eq16_4_*` aliases for (16.4) and (16.4)-(16.5). These aliases only name the proved factor/coordinate-transform surfaces; the real quasi-triangular block solve and floating-point stability rows remain open.
- Latest direct zero-coupling solve-wrapper wave: the shifted determinant/product-zero bridge now feeds active-block injectivity, surjectivity, bijectivity, trivial-kernel, unique-solve, nonsingular-inverse solution-identification, supplied two-column block-system construction, and previous-column uniqueness wrappers without carrying quasi-Schur block-map hypotheses. These are exact algebraic wrappers for the degenerate branch, not the genuine coupled real-Schur separation proof.
- Latest coupled block-action packaging wave: the genuinely coupled two-column route now has explicit block matrices for the left `A` action and the supplied `2 x 2` Schur-block action, plus a proved equivalence between the existing coupled `u,v` equations and equality of those two block actions on the concatenated vector. The product-shift no-eigenvector route can now consume a no-nonzero-block-action certificate directly; the remaining red bottleneck is still the spectral theorem deriving that certificate from common-complex-eigenvalue separation.
- Latest direct block-kernel separation bridge: the supplied adjacent two-column coefficient kernel is now proved equivalent to equality of the left `A` block action and the supplied `2 x 2` Schur-block action on the same concatenated vector. Consequently, a no-nonzero-block-action certificate directly gives determinant nonsingularity for the two-column coefficient. This removes the product-shift detour from the eventual spectral-separation route, but still leaves the common-complex-eigenvalue/intertwiner theorem open.
- Latest two-column intertwining bridge: the coupled active-column equations now also have the standard matrix form `A * U = U * J`, where `U` packages the two active columns and `J` is the supplied adjacent real `2 x 2` Schur block. This gives the next spectral proof a conventional intertwiner surface while still leaving the complex shared-eigenvalue transfer open.
- Latest complex intertwiner eigenvector bridge: a general finite complex-matrix theorem now proves that any intertwiner `A * X = X * B` maps a supplied `B` eigenvector to an `A` eigenvector with the same eigenvalue, with a companion existential eigenpair wrapper when the image is nonzero. This closes a reusable algebraic dependency for the future real-Schur block-separation proof; the still-open part is producing a suitable nonzero image from the genuine `2 x 2` block spectral hypotheses.
- Latest real-to-complex intertwining bridge: rectangular real matrices now have a reusable entrywise complexification map preserving multiplication and intertwining identities, and the two-column `A * U = U * J` bridge has a complexified wrapper ready for the finite complex intertwiner/eigenvector theorem.
- Latest intertwiner kernel-invariance bridge: a general real-matrix lemma now proves that `A * U = U * J` makes the kernel of `U` invariant under `J`, with a two-column Schur-block specialization. This is the algebraic setup for the remaining irreducibility/no-real-invariant-line argument in the genuine coupled block case.
- Latest no-real-eigenline kernel bridge: determinant algebra for two real `Fin 2` columns now proves that a nonzero real intertwiner `A * U = U * J` has trivial kernel whenever the right-hand `2 x 2` block has no real eigenvector, with a two-column Schur-block specialization. This closes the irreducible-real-kernel dependency and leaves the complexified nonzero-image transfer as the next proof-risk step toward the no-block-action certificate.
- Latest complex nonzero-image bridge: a trivial real-kernel theorem now lifts through entrywise complexification, proving nonzero complex vectors remain nonzero under the complexified column-pair map in the no-real-eigenvector `2 x 2` block setting. This closes the nonzero-image dependency needed before combining the complex intertwiner eigenpair bridge with a source-level no-common-spectrum hypothesis.
- Latest supplied complex-separation block bridge: a supplied complex eigenpair of the adjacent `2 x 2` block, a no-real-eigenline certificate, and a supplied exclusion of the same complex eigenvalue for `A` now prove the no-block-action certificate and hence determinant nonsingularity of the two-column coefficient. This composes the new kernel/nonzero-image algebra with the existing complex intertwiner bridge, but still treats the block eigenpair and separation data as explicit hypotheses.
- Latest complex-root block bridge: the adjacent `2 x 2` block now has a concrete complex root vector `(mu - T_qq, T_qp)`, proved nonzero when the subdiagonal is nonzero and proved to be an eigenvector from the supplied scalar characteristic-root equation. The determinant route can now consume a scalar complex root plus separation data instead of an explicit vector eigenpair.
- Latest negative-discriminant root bridge: the standard complex root `(T_pp + T_qq)/2 + i delta/2` is now proved to satisfy the adjacent `2 x 2` characteristic equation whenever `delta^2` equals the negative discriminant. The determinant route can now consume a supplied real square-root/discriminant certificate rather than an arbitrary complex scalar root.
- Latest no-real-line delta certificate: the same nonzero negative-discriminant square-root certificate now proves the adjacent `2 x 2` block has no real eigenvector, and the determinant route has a wrapper using this certificate directly. This removes a separate no-real-eigenline hypothesis from the supplied delta-root route.
- Latest determinant-shaped complex separation bridge: a nonzero shifted determinant of the complexified left block now rules out same-root complex eigenpairs of `A`, and the adjacent two-column determinant route consumes this determinant separation together with the nonzero negative-discriminant certificate. This replaces the remaining supplied `A` eigenpair-exclusion predicate with a determinant-facing hypothesis.
- Latest quasi-Schur determinant-shaped separation adapters: same-block quasi-Schur block-map data now packages the adjacent-block zero pattern together with the determinant-shaped complex separation route, including a no-block-action wrapper and determinant consequence. The direct discriminant variant uses `sqrt (-disc)` and derives both the nonzero square-root and `T_qp != 0` from `disc < 0`, but it still requires the shifted complex determinant separation for `A` as an explicit certificate.
- Latest direct negative-discriminant helpers: `disc < 0` now directly supplies the nonzero subdiagonal fact, the no-real-eigenline certificate, the no-block-action certificate, and the determinant-shaped complex separation route using `sqrt (-disc)`. The same-block quasi-Schur wrapper now delegates to this direct bridge, leaving only the source construction of `disc < 0` and the shifted determinant separation open.
- Latest irreducible-block discriminant converse: a nonnegative discriminant for the adjacent real `2 x 2` block now constructs a concrete real eigenline, and the contrapositive proves `disc < 0` from a no-real-eigenline certificate. This gives the future real-Schur export another route: prove same-block irreducibility/no real eigenline, then derive the discriminant certificate needed by the separation predicate.
- Latest no-real-eigenline separation producers: a supplied no-real-eigenline certificate plus the shifted determinant separation now directly packages both the explicit real-Schur block-separation predicate and the bundled real-quasi-Schur predicate. This removes the need for future callers to separately pass `disc < 0` once the stronger real-Schur construction exports irreducibility of the adjacent block.
- Latest source irreducible-plane helper/export: the nonreal branch of the real invariant-subspace peel now has a local theorem proving that its rotation-scaling invariant plane has no real eigenline, an exact-dimension invariant-subspace export retains that no-real-eigenline certificate in the two-dimensional branch, and a source-local `MatrixNoRealEigenline` predicate plus `principalTwoBlock` vocabulary and canonical rotation-scaling `2 x 2` theorem give `RealQuasiSchur` vocabulary for future block exports without importing Sylvester files. The same source layer now also proves that any real `2 x 2` matrix, or principal `2 x 2` block, with no real eigenline has negative discriminant, and `RealQuasiSchur` now transports a no-real-eigenline invariant plane across an orthogonal column frame to the corresponding principal block of `Q^T A Q`, including the direct negative-discriminant corollary, the `d = 2` frame-span adapter used by `exists_orthogonal_frame`, an existential wrapper that frames any two-dimensional no-real-eigenline invariant subspace with leading block certificates, a peel-level one-or-two wrapper whose two-dimensional branch already carries those frame certificates, leading-block preservation through the trailing recursive conjugation, trailing-side `Sum.inr` split/block-conjugation, entrywise, principal-block, and no-real-eigenline/negative-discriminant certificate transport from the recursive block, a one-step wrapper that frames a two-dimensional peel and re-embeds it through an orthogonal trailing factor while retaining the leading certificate, and a public `HasRealQuasiSchurTwoBlockSpectral` predicate with a trailing parent-block-map lift plus the enriched `real_quasi_schur_blocks_twoBlockSpectral` API. This preserves the source-side irreducibility fact through the constructed Schur recursion; Sylvester separation still needs the shifted determinant/no-common-spectrum side.
- Latest real-Schur block-separation predicate: `IsSylvesterTwoColumnRealSchurBlockSeparation` records the concrete supplied certificates (`disc < 0` and shifted complex determinant separation at `sqrt (-disc)`), and named wrappers now derive the no-block-action and determinant-nonsingularity conclusions from that predicate. The constructed real quasi-Schur API now supplies the no-real-eigenline/negative-discriminant side for adjacent same-block `2 x 2` blocks; `sylvesterTwoColumnRealQuasiSchurBlockSeparation_of_twoBlockSpectral_det_separation` packages it with the still-explicit shifted determinant separation, and `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_block_and_det_ne_zero_of_twoBlockSpectral_det_separation` immediately returns the adjacent-block predicate plus determinant nonsingularity.
- Latest no-common complex-eigenpair route: `finiteComplexMatrix_det_sub_scalar_ne_zero_of_no_eigenpair` proves the finite complex converse from no supplied eigenpair at a scalar to shifted determinant nonsingularity. `sylvesterTwoColumnRealSchurBlockComplexRoot_det_separation_of_disc_no_common_complex_eigenpair` uses the constructed complex root eigenpair of a negative-discriminant adjacent block plus a global no-common-complex-eigenpair hypothesis to supply the shifted determinant certificate, and `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_block_and_det_ne_zero_of_twoBlockSpectral_no_common_complex_eigenpair` feeds that route through the constructed `HasRealQuasiSchurTwoBlockSpectral` API. The remaining source gap is proving the global no-common complex spectral hypothesis automatically.
- Latest complex Schur diagonal-separation adapter: `complex_det_ne_zero_of_upperTriangular_diag_ne_zero`, `complexShiftedCoeff_upperTriangular`, `complexShiftedCoeff_det_ne_zero_of_upperTriangular_diag_ne`, and `complexSylvester_shift_det_ne_zero_of_schur_diagonal_separation` now convert pairwise separation of supplied complex Schur diagonal entries into the shifted determinant hypotheses used by the exact complex Bartels-Stewart solve. `complexSylvester_exists_unique_of_schur_diagonal_separation` packages this into the complex Schur-factor solve surface; the vec/Kronecker determinant product is now tracked by the direct complex triangular coefficient entry below.
- Latest complex vec/Kronecker determinant product: `complexSylvesterVecCoeff` defines the complex coefficient `I_n kron A - B^T kron I_m`, `complexSylvesterVecCoeff_reindex_upperTriangular` proves it is triangular after reversing the block coordinate, and `complexSylvesterVecCoeff_det_eq_prod_of_upperTriangular` proves the supplied complex triangular determinant formula `prod_{j,i} (A_ii - B_jj)`. The iff theorem `complexSylvesterVecCoeff_det_ne_zero_iff_of_upperTriangular_diagonal_separation` and corollary `complexSylvesterVecCoeff_det_ne_zero_of_upperTriangular_diagonal_separation` identify nonsingularity with pairwise diagonal separation, and `complexUpperTriangular_exists_eigenpair_diag` plus `complexUpperTriangular_diagonal_separation_of_no_common_eigenpair` now convert a no-common supplied eigenpair hypothesis for triangular factors into that diagonal separation. The endpoint `complexSylvesterVecCoeff_det_ne_zero_of_upperTriangular_no_common_eigenpair` and source-numbered aliases `H16_eq16_2_complexSylvesterVecCoeff` / `H16_eq16_3_complexSylvesterVecCoeff_*` expose the (16.2)-(16.3) supplied triangular spectral route. The full unsupplied nondiagonal Kronecker spectral equivalence remains open.
- Latest complex Schur no-common-eigenpair solve route: `complexSchurFactor_eigenpair_to_original` transports right eigenpairs of supplied unitary Schur factors back to the original matrices, `complexSchur_diagonal_separation_of_no_common_eigenpair` derives Schur diagonal separation from a no-common-right-eigenpair hypothesis on the original complex matrices, and `complexSylvester_exists_unique_of_schur_no_common_eigenpair` packages the exact complex Sylvester unique-solve theorem under that source-facing hypothesis. This closes the supplied Schur-factor exact solve route from no common right eigenpair; it still does not transfer the full vec/Kronecker determinant through arbitrary Schur similarities or specialize the real coefficient automatically.
- Latest unconditional complex no-common-eigenpair solve route: `complexSylvester_exists_unique_of_no_common_eigenpair` now obtains the complex Schur factors by existence and proves exact unique solvability of `A X - X B = C` directly from a no-common supplied right-eigenpair hypothesis on the original complex matrices. The source-numbered alias `H16_eq16_3_complexSylvester_exists_unique_of_no_common_eigenpair` exposes the (16.3)-(16.6) map. - Latest rotation-scaling block bridge: canonical real `2 x 2` entries `[[alpha,beta],[-beta,alpha]]` with `beta != 0` now prove the negative discriminant needed by the real-Schur block-separation predicate, and package that algebra into the bundled real-quasi-Schur predicate when the usual block-map data and shifted determinant separation are supplied. ## Reused from Repository or Mathlib

| Source concept/result | Existing declaration | File/module |
|---|---|---|
| Legacy square matrix product | `matMul` | `LeanFpAnalysis.FP.Analysis.MatrixAlgebra` |
| Rectangular matrix product | `matMulRect`, `rectMatMul` | `LeanFpAnalysis.FP.Analysis.MatrixAlgebra` |
| Frobenius norm and squared norm | `frobNorm`, `frobNormSq`, `frobNorm_matMul_le`, triangle/subtraction lemmas | `LeanFpAnalysis.FP.Analysis.MatrixAlgebra` |
| Orthogonality and norm invariance | `IsOrthogonal`, `frobNormSq_orthogonal_left`, `frobNormSq_orthogonal_right` | `LeanFpAnalysis.FP.Analysis.MatrixAlgebra` |
| Transpose | `matTranspose` | `LeanFpAnalysis.FP.Analysis.MatrixAlgebra` |
| Column-stacking vectorization and Kronecker products | `Matrix.vec`, `Matrix.kronecker`, `Matrix.kronecker_mulVec_vec`, `Matrix.vec_mul_eq_mulVec` | `Mathlib.LinearAlgebra.Matrix.Vec` |
| Finite vector max norm for product-index vectors | Mathlib finite-function norm with `norm_le_pi_norm` and `pi_norm_le_iff_of_nonneg` | imported through existing Mathlib/Matrix infrastructure |

Latest open-row update:
- For the degenerate two-column quasi-triangular block route, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_block_and_det_ne_zero_of_quasiSchur_shifted_det_product_zero` now combines same-block quasi-Schur block-map data with nonsingular shifted column coefficients and the zero coupling-product certificate, yielding both `IsAdjacentQuasiTriangularBlockFn` and determinant nonsingularity for the active two-column coefficient. The underlying direct zero-coupling determinant route now also has active-block solve and nonsingular-inverse block-system wrappers through the `*_of_shifted_det_product_zero` family, and the same zero-coupling route with quasi-Schur provenance is exposed through the `*_of_quasiSchur_shifted_det_product_zero` family. This closes the zero-coupling adapter/solve subcase; the genuinely coupled real-Schur 2x2 route still needs the no-coupled-action/product-shift determinant certificate from structural separation.
- For (16.4)-(16.8), `sylvester_realQuasiSchur_factors` exposes the existing real quasi-Schur decomposition surface directly in the Chapter 16 Sylvester file, and `sylvesterTriangularShiftedCoeff_*`, `existsUnique_sylvester_triangular_column_step_of_shifted_det`, and `sylvester_triangular_column_step_eq_of_shifted_det` now package nonsingular shifted triangular column coefficients as exact inverse, injectivity, surjectivity, bijectivity, unique-solve, active column-step, and column-step equality facts. The row remains open because the real quasi-triangular Bartels-Stewart solve and its floating-point error propagation are not assembled from these supplied certificates.
- For the two-column quasi-triangular block route, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_det_ne_zero_of_rightInverse`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_mulVec_surjective_of_rightInverse`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_det_ne_zero_of_leftInverse`, and `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_mulVec_bijective_of_rightInverse_leftInverse` close determinant/surjectivity/bijectivity consequences of supplied inverse certificates. The quasi-Schur/no-coupled determinant bridge now also has direct active-block injectivity, surjectivity, bijectivity, trivial-kernel, unique-solve, and nonsingular-inverse solution-identification wrappers. The missing step is still deriving the no-coupled-action/product-shift determinant certificate from structural separation hypotheses for genuine real-Schur 2x2 blocks.
- For (16.2), entrywise gap assumptions now feed determinant nonsingularity for diagonal and supplied Schur-diagonal Sylvester coefficients and diagonal/supplied spectral Lyapunov coefficients; determinant plus concrete-left-inverse finite-op-norm certificates feed vectorized bijectivity plus unique-solve wrappers for finite, Sylvester, and Lyapunov coefficients; and supplied `SepLowerBound` or positive exact-`sylvesterSepInf` lower bounds now feed concrete Sylvester/Lyapunov vec-coefficient sigma-min, determinant, left/right nonsingular-inverse action, and solution-identification certificates. This closes another source-to-coefficient certificate bridge but not the fully general nondiagonal Kronecker spectral criterion.

## Hidden-Hypothesis Summary

- The existing proved square theorems assume explicit Frobenius-norm bounds, `SepLowerBound`, nonzero norm-squared hypotheses where needed, and supplied linearized equations. These are domain/reused-theorem assumptions, not replacements for the target equation.
- `sylvesterSepInf` records the exact infimum object for `sep(A,B)`; `SepLowerBound` is now equivalent to a positive lower bound of that infimum when the feasible ratio set is nonempty, and the feasible set is proved nonempty in positive dimension. The printed minimum form is closed in positive dimension by `exists_sylvesterSep_minimizer`, `isLeast_sylvesterSepRatios`, and `exists_sylvesterSep_ratio_minimizer`.
- `sylvesterBackwardErrorInf` records the backward-error eta quantity as an infimum of nonnegative feasible `IsBackwardError` certificates. The two-sided xi bridge and least-value attainment are proved for this infimum model under the stated positive-weight and nonempty-feasible-set hypotheses, and the SVD optimal-perturbation construction now discharges nonemptiness in `exists_sylvesterBackwardError_minimizer_of_svdOptimalPerturbations`, `sylvesterBackwardErrorInf_mem_sylvesterBackwardErrorValues_of_svdOptimalPerturbations`, and `isLeast_sylvesterBackwardErrorValues_of_svdOptimalPerturbations`.
- `lyapunovBackwardErrorInf` records the Lyapunov-specific eta quantity as an infimum over structured certificates with one tied `DeltaA` perturbation and symmetric `DeltaC`. The two-sided Lyapunov eta/xi bridge and least-value attainment are proved under the stated positive-weight and nonempty-feasible-set hypotheses, with the symmetric-spectral optimizer discharging nonemptiness.
- `LyapunovConditionFirstOrderBound` is an explicit condition-number certificate corresponding to (16.27). A positive `SepLowerBound(A, -A^T)` supplies a safe source-facing Lyapunov condition wrapper via `M = 1/sigma`, with the raw inequality exposed by `lyapunov_first_order_bound_of_sepLowerBound`; a positive lower bound on the exact `sylvesterSepInf A (-A^T)` model supplies both the predicate-level wrapper `lyapunovCond_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf_isLyapunovConditionFirstOrderBound`, the raw wrapper `lyapunov_first_order_bound_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf`, and the theorem-level wrapper `H16_eq16_27_lyapunov_condition_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf`; a positive sigma-min lower bound on the Lyapunov operator supplies the same wrapper via `lyapunovInverseOpBound_of_sigmaMin`, with the raw inequality exposed by `lyapunov_first_order_bound_of_sigmaMin`; a positive lower-bound certificate for the concrete `lyapunovVecCoeff` supplies it via `lyapunovCond_of_vecCoeff_sigmaMin_isLyapunovConditionFirstOrderBound`; a concrete left inverse plus finite operator-2 bound supplies it via `lyapunov_first_order_bound_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` and `lyapunov_relative_first_order_bound_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le`; a finite Gram eigenvalue lower bound supplies the concrete coefficient/operator lower bound and direct source wrapper via `lyapunovVecCoeff_sigmaMin_of_gram_eigenvalues`, `lyapunovOp_sigmaMin_of_vecCoeff_gram_eigenvalues`, and `H16_eq16_27_lyapunov_condition_of_vecCoeff_gram_eigenvalues`; diagonal entrywise separation supplies such a Gram-eigenvalue lower bound via `lyapunovVecCoeff_diagonal_gram_eigenvalues_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge`; and supplied orthogonal spectral-diagonal data supplies `sep(A,-A^T)` lower-bound/infimum certificates, operator, coefficient, Gram, and source-shaped relative perturbation bounds via `SepLowerBound_lyapunovSpectralDiagonal_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterSepInf_lyapunovSpectralDiagonal_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterSepInf_lyapunovSpectralDiagonal_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge_of_pos_dim`, `lyapunovOp_sigmaMin_spectralDiagonal_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `lyapunovVecCoeff_spectralDiagonal_sigmaMin_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `lyapunovVecCoeff_spectralDiagonal_gram_eigenvalues_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `H16_eq16_27_lyapunov_condition_spectralDiagonal_of_vecCoeff_entrywise_abs_ge`, and `H16_eq16_27_lyapunov_condition_spectralDiagonal_of_sep_entrywise_abs_ge`. The remaining exact displayed nondiagonal construction is proving the concrete Gram spectral value or lower bound automatically without assuming supplied spectral factors.
- The Lyapunov perturbation wrappers from `SepLowerBound` and exact-infimum certificates reuse the existing Sylvester perturbation theorem with `B = -A^T` and `DeltaB = -DeltaA^T`, proving the required norm bound for the transposed perturbation explicitly. They keep the nonzero `frobNormSq DeltaX` and nonzero/positive `frobNorm X` assumptions visible because those are premises of the older absolute/relative perturbation theorems.
- `sylvester_schur_transform_identity`, `sylvester_schur_transform_solution_iff`, `existsUnique_isSylvesterSolutionRect_schurDiagonal`, `sylvesterVecCoeff_schurDiagonal_det_ne_zero`, `sylvesterOp_sigmaMin_schurDiagonal_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterVecCoeff_schurDiagonal_sigmaMin_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterVecCoeff_schurDiagonal_gram_eigenvalues_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `SepLowerBound_schurDiagonal_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterSepInf_schurDiagonal_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterSepInf_schurDiagonal_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge_of_pos_dim`, `existsUnique_isSylvesterSolutionRect_schurTriangular`, and the `sylvesterVecCoeff_schurTriangular_*` vectorized coefficient theorems assume supplied factorizations and orthogonality; the triangular theorems also assume a supplied upper-triangular factor and nonsingular shifted column coefficients. `sylvester_realQuasiSchur_factors` records real quasi-Schur factor existence, but does not combine that factorization with the solve recurrence. `sylvester_quasiTriangular_two_column_block_system_of_solution`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockRhs`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockSystem_of_rightInverse_columns`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockSystem_columns_eq_of_leftInverse`, the two-column determinant/surjectivity/bijectivity wrappers, the determinant-based nonsingular-inverse wrappers, the determinant previous-column uniqueness wrappers, and the nonsingular-inverse previous-column solve/uniqueness wrappers assume a supplied adjacent 2x2 quasi-triangular block shape and/or supplied determinant/inverse certificates for its exact two-column block coefficient data. These are not proofs of structural quasi-triangular block nonsingularity from spectral separation, Hessenberg-Schur reductions, or floating-point stability.
- `SylvesterPsiFirstOrderBound` is an explicit condition-number certificate corresponding to (16.24). The `sqrt 3 * Psi * epsilon` relative perturbation theorem is proved from that certificate, and a positive `SepLowerBound` supplies a safe source-facing `Psi` wrapper via `M = 1/sigma`, with the raw inequality exposed by `sylvester_first_order_bound_of_sepLowerBound`; a positive lower bound on the exact `sylvesterSepInf` model supplies both the predicate-level wrapper `sylvesterPsi_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf_isPsiFirstOrderBound`, the raw wrapper `sylvester_first_order_bound_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf`, and the theorem-level wrapper `H16_eq16_24_structured_condition_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf`; a positive sigma-min lower bound on the Sylvester operator supplies the same wrapper via `sylvesterInverseOpBound_of_sigmaMin`, with the raw inequality exposed by `sylvester_first_order_bound_of_sigmaMin`; a positive lower-bound certificate for the concrete `sylvesterVecCoeff` supplies it via `sylvesterPsi_of_vecCoeff_sigmaMin_isPsiFirstOrderBound`, with raw wrappers for sigma-min and finite Gram-eigenvalue lower bounds; and a concrete left inverse plus `finiteOpNorm2Le` bound supplies it via `sylvesterPsi_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le_isPsiFirstOrderBound`, with the raw inequality exposed by `sylvester_first_order_bound_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le`. **Progress (Split-3B Claude lane, `Analysis/InverseOpNorm2.lean`, import-only):** the spectral core `||P^{-1}||_2 = 1/sigma_min` is proved unconditionally by `rayleigh_lower_bound_of_le_finiteHermitianEigenvalues`, `sigmaMin_mul_vecNorm2_le_matMulVec`, and `vecNorm2_le_inv_sigmaMin_mul_matMulVec`. `Higham16VecNorm.lean` closes the Frobenius/`vec` norm bridge, proves a product-index finite Gram identity and lower-bound bridge, transfers finite Gram eigenvalue lower bounds to the concrete Sylvester and Lyapunov coefficient/operator hypotheses, exposes direct Gram-eigenvalue wrappers for (16.23)-(16.25), (16.27), and (16.28), supplies diagonal plus supplied Schur-diagonal Gram-eigenvalue certificates from coordinate separation, adds a concrete left-inverse route to Sylvester/Lyapunov coefficient sigma-min, Gram, inverse-operator, source-shaped condition, and raw first-order wrappers, and now transfers supplied source `SepLowerBound`/exact-infimum lower-bound certificates into concrete Sylvester/Lyapunov coefficient sigma-min and determinant certificates. The remaining full self-supply gap is constructing/bounding such an inverse certificate automatically for arbitrary nondiagonal coefficients without supplied diagonal factors.
- The general Sylvester concrete-left-inverse and source-sep routes use explicit finite-dimensional certificates rather than proving the full eigenvalue criterion. `SepLowerBound_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` transfers a supplied left inverse and finite operator-2 bound for `sylvesterVecCoeff n n A B` to `SepLowerBound n A B (1 / M)`, while `sylvesterVecCoeff_sigmaMin_of_sepLowerBound` and `sylvesterVecCoeff_det_ne_zero_of_sepLowerBound` transfer a supplied source `SepLowerBound` back to the concrete coefficient sigma-min/determinant routes. The exact-infimum variants use `SepLowerBound_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf` and keep positivity hypotheses visible.
- The current concrete-left-inverse and source-sep Lyapunov routes use explicit finite-dimensional certificates rather than assuming the desired (16.27) condition-number theorem: `lyapunovOp_sigmaMin_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` transfers the left inverse to an operator sigma-min lower bound, `SepLowerBound_lyapunov_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` transfers it to a safe `sep(A,-A^T)` certificate, `sylvesterSepInf_lyapunov_ge_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` exposes the corresponding exact-infimum lower bound in positive dimension, `lyapunov_perturbation_bound_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` / `lyapunov_relative_perturbation_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` instantiate the absolute and relative perturbation inequalities, and `lyapunovVecCoeff_mulVec_bijective_of_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` / `existsUnique_lyapunovVecCoeff_mulVec_of_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` expose the matching vectorized solve certificates. Conversely, `lyapunovVecCoeff_sigmaMin_of_sepLowerBound` and `lyapunovVecCoeff_det_ne_zero_of_sepLowerBound` transfer supplied `sep(A,-A^T)` lower-bound certificates back into the concrete Lyapunov vec-coefficient routes.
- The current direct sigma-min Lyapunov route also keeps its certificate visible: `SepLowerBound_lyapunov_of_sigmaMin` converts a positive lower bound for the Lyapunov operator into a `sep(A,-A^T)` lower bound, `sylvesterSepInf_lyapunov_ge_of_sigmaMin` transfers it to the exact infimum model in positive dimension, and `lyapunov_perturbation_bound_of_sigmaMin`, `lyapunov_first_order_bound_of_sigmaMin`, and `lyapunov_relative_perturbation_of_sigmaMin` instantiate the same source-shaped first-order inequalities. This does not prove the exact nondiagonal spectral value of the Lyapunov coefficient automatically.
- The explicit solution-witness wrappers strengthen the user-facing certificate surface but keep the same hypotheses visible: determinant, sigma-min, finite-Gram, or concrete-left-inverse data. `existsUnique_finiteMatrix_nonsingInv_mulVec_solution_of_det_ne_zero` and its Sylvester/Lyapunov wrappers prove both the coefficient equation and `x = P^{-1} c` for the unique witness; they do not supply the missing general spectral criterion or construct a coefficient inverse automatically.
- The source-sep/exact-infimum solution-witness wrappers add the same explicit bijectivity, nonsingular-inverse witness, left/right action, and solution-identification surface when the caller supplies `SepLowerBound` or a positive lower bound on `sylvesterSepInf`. They use the proved source-to-coefficient determinant bridge and still keep the separation certificate visible.
- The (16.29) practical-bound theorems assume visible certificates: a left inverse `Pinv * sylvesterVecCoeff = 1`, an entrywise inverse bound `|Pinv| <= PinvAbs`, and an `IsSylvesterComputedResidualBudget` certificate. The residual-budget certificate can be produced from an explicit residual error matrix `dR` with `Rhat = R + dR` and `|dR| <= Ru`; the floating-point residual model now supplies that certificate for arbitrary `A,B` through `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_left_inverse` and its scalar/monotone variants when inverse certificates are supplied. For square coefficients, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_vecCoeff_det_ne_zero`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_vecCoeff_gram_eigenvalues`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_vecCoeff_sigmaMin`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_sepLowerBound`, and `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf` plus their scalar/monotone variants use proved determinant certificates to instantiate the nonsingular inverse and its entrywise absolute-value budget. The non-floating certificate and explicit error-model theorem families similarly have determinant-nonzero square endpoints. The monotone practical wrapper assumes componentwise larger estimated inverse/residual/rounding budgets and proves only the corresponding larger error bound; it is not a proof of a LAPACK estimator. The diagonal, supplied Schur-diagonal, supplied Schur-triangular, separated-diagonal, source-`SepLowerBound`, and exact-infimum floating-point scalar wrappers additionally assume a scalar cap on the already-defined practical budget vector; they do not derive an estimator. The supplied Schur-diagonal and Schur-triangular wrappers discharge the left-inverse and entrywise inverse-bound certificates from proved determinant-nonsingularity theorems for supplied orthogonal factors; the triangular wrappers also assume a supplied upper-triangular factor and shifted diagonal nonsingularity conditions. They still assume the supplied Schur-style data and a computed-residual certificate/error model. They do not prove rounded Schur solve arithmetic, quasi-triangular block handling, or the LAPACK estimator.
- The non-floating practical-bound source wrappers now mirror the floating-point source wrappers for `SepLowerBound` and exact-infimum certificates across computed-residual certificates, raw budgets, and explicit residual-error models, with scalar/monotone variants. They reuse determinant/nonsingular-inverse bridges and do not change the estimator or rounded-solve assumptions.
- No new global axioms, `sorry`, `admit`, `unsafe`, or opaque placeholders are introduced by the Chapter 16 companion module.
